LEX   (MARY) := S/(S\NP)
        : (LAM P (P CAT))
LEX   (KNOWS) := (S\*NP)/^S
        : (LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW X) S)))
LEX   (JOHN) := S/(S\NP)
        : (LAM P (P DOG))
LEX   (LOVES) := (S\*NP)/^NP
        : (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))
LEX   (MARY) := (S\NP)\((S\NP)/NP)
        : (LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X)))
<     (LOVES)(MARY) := S\NP
        : ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X))))
>     (JOHN)(LOVES MARY) := S
        : ((LAM P (P DOG))
           ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))))
>     (KNOWS)(JOHN LOVES MARY) := S\*NP
        : ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW X) S)))
           ((LAM P (P DOG))
            ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X))))))
>     (MARY)(KNOWS JOHN LOVES MARY) := S
        : ((LAM P (P CAT))
           ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW X) S)))
            ((LAM P (P DOG))
             ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))))))

Final LF, normal-order evaluated: 

    ((KNOW CAT) ((MARY (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))) DOG)) =
    (KNOW CAT (MARY (\ X . \ Y . LOVE Y X) DOG))

LEX   (KNOWS) := (S\*NP)/^S
        : (LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW S) X)))
LEX   (JOHN) := S/(S\NP)
        : (LAM P (P JOHN))
LEX   (LOVES) := (S\*NP)/^NP
        : (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))
LEX   (MARY) := (S\NP)\((S\NP)/NP)
        : (LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X)))
<     (LOVES)(MARY) := S\NP
        : ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X))))
>     (JOHN)(LOVES MARY) := S
        : ((LAM P (P JOHN))
           ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))))
>     (KNOWS)(JOHN LOVES MARY) := S\*NP
        : ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW S) X)))
           ((LAM P (P JOHN))
            ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X))))))
>     (MARY)(KNOWS JOHN LOVES MARY) := S
        : ((LAM P (P MARY))
           ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW S) X)))
            ((LAM P (P JOHN))
             ((LAM P (LAM X ((MARY P) X))) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))))))

Final LF, normal-order evaluated: 

    ((KNOW ((MARY (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE Y) X)))) JOHN)) MARY) =
    (KNOW (MARY (\ X . \ Y . LOVE Y X) JOHN) MARY)

LEX   (MARY) := S/(S\NP)
        : (LAM P (P MARY))
LEX   (LOVES) := (S\*NP)/^NP
        : (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE X) Y)))
LEX   (JOHN) := (S\NP)\((S\NP)/NP)
        : (LAM P (P JOHN))
<     (LOVES)(JOHN) := S\NP
        : ((LAM P (P JOHN)) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE X) Y))))
>     (MARY)(LOVES JOHN) := S
        : ((LAM P (P MARY)) ((LAM P (P JOHN)) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE X) Y)))))
>     (KNOWS)(MARY LOVES JOHN) := S\*NP
        : ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW X) S)))
           ((LAM P (P MARY)) ((LAM P (P JOHN)) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE X) Y))))))
>     (JOHN)(KNOWS MARY LOVES JOHN) := S
        : ((LAM P (P DOG))
           ((LAM S (LAM X ((KNOW X) S)))
            ((LAM P (P MARY)) ((LAM P (P JOHN)) (LAM X (LAM Y ((LOVE X) Y)))))))

Final LF, normal-order evaluated: 

    ((KNOW DOG) ((LOVE JOHN) MARY)) =
    (KNOW DOG (LOVE JOHN MARY))
